 - ~~[‚ñ∂](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vBnVrVKLvYY&t=1456)~~  buy everything in an envelope, they put it in a closed format, everyone hands over envelopes with the inscription How much they will pay Well, or right away with the money, then one of them wins, Who has the most money in the envelope to everyone else  the money is returned, but the thing is that he does n‚Äôt have to return anything, then this is called the father of the first price.  - ~~[‚ñ∂](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vBnVrVKLvYY&t=1518)~~  equilibrium behavior.
